358:["$","li",null,{"style":{"marginBottom":"0.35em","fontSize":"1rem"},"children":"The TD(0) critic is the policy-evaluation step; the policy-gradient actor is the policy-improvement step. Both are \"partial\": the critic does one bootstrapped step rather than a full evaluation, and the actor takes a gradient nudge rather than a full greedy max. If the critic is far faster than the actor it tracks the policy well (stable but slow); if the actor is faster it improves against a stale, inaccurate value estimate, which destabilizes training — hence the two-timescale rule that the critic should adapt faster than the actor."}]
